<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закреплять.html>закрепля́ть</a> (21023)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрепить.html>закрепи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zakrepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закреплять.html>закрепля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakrepljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрепить.html>закрепи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fasten, to secure, to fix, to attach, to mount, to anchor</li>
<li>to consolidate, to strengthen</li>
<li>to allot</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:крепнуть.html>кре́п</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ля́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:закрепить.html>закрепи́ть</a>.

***закрутить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́ть</a> (9702)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крутить.html>крути́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krutítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakrutítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крутить.html>крути́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закручивать.html>закру́чивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to twirl, to twist, to wind around
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спина.html>спи́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakrutítʹ</b> komú-libo rúki za spínu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to twist someone's arms behind his back</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вожжа.html>во́жжи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakrutítʹ</b> vóžži na rúki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wind the reins round one's hands</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ус.html>усы́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakrutítʹ</b> usý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn up the ends of one's moustache; twirl/twiddle/twist one's moustache</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тер</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пыль.html>пыль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">véter <b>zakrutíl</b> pylʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the wind is stirring up the dust</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:роман.html>рома́н</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakrutítʹ</b> román (s)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to have/start an affair (with)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(tap etc)</i> to turn off, <i>(nut etc)</i> to turn tight, to tighten <i>(up)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гайка.html>га́йки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zakrutítʹ gájki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tighten the screws <i>(on someone)</i></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zakrutítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутиться.html>закрути́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakrutítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">закру́чиваться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to twist, to become twisted</li>
<li>to become screwed up</li>
<li>to begin to turn</li>
<li>to be tied up with one's affairs, to be bound up in one's affairs</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zakrutítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закру́ченный</a> (9702)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закру́ченный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakrúčennyj</span>)
</p>

***закручивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закручивать.html>закру́чивать</a> (23871)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zakrutítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закручивать.html>закру́чивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakrúčivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to twirl, to twist, to wind round
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закручивать.html>закру́чивать</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спина.html>спи́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakrúčivatʹ</b> komú-libo rúki za spínu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to twist someone's arms behind his back</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закручивать.html>закру́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вожжа.html>во́жжи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakrúčivatʹ</b> vóžži na rúki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wind the reins round one's hands</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закручивать.html>закру́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ус.html>усы́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakrúčivatʹ</b> usý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn up the ends of one's moustache; twirl/twiddle/twist one's moustache</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(tap etc)</i> to turn off, <i>(nut etc)</i> to turn tight, to tighten <i>(up)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закручивать.html>закру́чивать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гайка.html>га́йки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zakrúčivatʹ gájki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tighten the screws <i>(on someone)</i></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>кры́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ться</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 12a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:закрываться.html>закрыва́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>за-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-кры-</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закряхтеть.html>закряхте́ть</a> (23517)</h1><br><hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
